That church rocked! The last time I went there was back N January 2009. Wish I was still attending, & still hearing the attendees cry out to the Most High! I also wish I lived Nx door to the house of the Lord. I miss it, & hopefully I will find a way to get back to that wonderful, glorious house of God! I became a member of Antioch back N May 2008, & I was real proud of it. My former Sister N Law found out by saying "Oh, I didn't know you joined Antioch, that's good". When I first attended it back N April 2008, i was given papers to fill out, & when the pastor told us to go around & say hello to everyone, the song " we're blessed N the city (we are blessed) was playing. My stepniece was baptized there. The band can really rock the hooouuussse! Wayne & Myesha Chaney R really awesome folks.
What I also miss, that @ the end of the service, while the pastor was speaking, his wife sang "choose life" N the background. The day before my 30th cake day, there was a saxophonist getting down performing the same tune! Because of that, I just want to revive those days.</review>

Ordered flowers for delivery to my girlfriend on St. Valentine's Day. Purchased the 'Perfect Dozen' and upgraded to premium, which added $30 to the arrangement which "[they'll] add more blooms and select the highest quality flowers we offer in this style." The Deluxe upgrade "Additional flowers will be added to enhance the bouquet." Well, no additional flowers were added, 4 of the dozen were already wilting pretty bad, then my girlfriend noticed there was hardly any water in the large vase, maybe a quarter to half a cup of water. Photo shows Eucalyptus Baby Blue in it but there was none, just a lot of leather fern and lemon leaf, and seeded eucalyptus along with gold glitter curly sticks. Overall, spent almost $150 on a $80 quality arrangement. I picked this place because it had the highest rating in the area, but that's not true at all.</text>

<Review>SVC is by far the worst motorcycle dealer in Ventura County, if not all of Southern California.  Their parts department does not carry a large inventory insuring that their customers will have to wait.  Their service department is staffed by young, untrained technicians who perform shoddy work.

I purchased a motorcycle from them in 2001.  Two years later it developed an intermittent missing problem and I brought it to them under warranty.  They tried on three separate occasions to find and repair the problem and couldn't.  They ended up giving the bike back to me un-repaired.  I then brought the bike to a competing dealer who diagnosed and located the problem in 10 minutes, ordered the part and returned my motorcycle in three days.

While SVC had my motorcycle the last time under warranty, they kept it for 4 weeks, broke my carburetor float bowls, glued them back together with epoxy, replaced defective parts with used ones, stored it outside in the rain (customary for them) and they returned the motorcycle to me completely filthy and corroded.  They refused to repair the damage they had caused or even detail the bike.

I highly recommend that you avoid Simi Valley Cycles.< /Review></record>

<Review>My name is Miguel, and I am an Internal Medicine Resident (PGY-1 categorical) at Fairview Hospital of Cleveland Clinic, Ohio.
As an IMG and applicant to a medical residency training program here in the United States, I was looking for clinical rotations last year. I was fortunate to have found California Heart and Vein Clinic to rotate.

During my rotation through Dr Chane‚Äôs clinic, I learned how to put the theoretical concepts into the practice of cardiology. And beyond the clinical aspects, I also learned how to lead an exceptional healthcare team and to optimize time during busy schedules.

Academically, we reviewed and discussed journal articles on current progresses in cardiology, as well as topics presented in congresses like the World Congress of Cardiology and the European Society of Cardiology. I had access to the current issues of the Journal of the American College of Cardiology (JACC) and other resources. Dr Chane helped me fine-tune my presentation abilities and grasp the most important concepts of the topics presented. I had the opportunity to write an article about one of the topics I presented; Dr Chane reviewed the article and we submitted it to a medical journal. Another very remarkable aspect of my academical training during this rotation, was learning to read echocardiograms and nuclear cardiac imaging in order to make a diagnoses.

What an excellent experience it was to shadow Dr. Chane! It was critical for my matching. The outstanding letter of recommendation he gave me added significant weight to my application.

< review>
After years of walking buy Pizza Guys I finally got around to giving them a try.
I walked in and ordered a extra large California garlic chicken pizza, comes with a free liter of soda.
I was told it would take about 15 min. ‚Äú no worries I‚Äôve got time, I walked next door a talked with Angie, the Happy Doughnuts owner‚Äù about 20 min later the pizza was ready and was handed to me. ‚Äú for an extra large it feels kind of lite, I said to my self‚Äù When I got home I opened the box and looked at the pizza for the first time. My initial impression was that it looks really good, I grabbed a slice and it folded over in all it‚Äôs soggyness. (1star) The taste? Solid 2.5 stars out of 5 ‚Äúmediocre‚Äù  Value? 1 star, way over priced, I ate 3/4 of it by myself ‚Äúkeep in mind it‚Äôs an extra large‚Äù I can buy a large pizza from one of my favorite pizzerias for less and only eat 3 slices and the taste?, for-get-about-it! ‚ÄúIf you know what I mean‚Äù

<review>Just good pizza.

I've only been here once, but I expect that I will go again (and update this review accordingly).

Pizza Guys makes good pizza.  They have several specialty pizzas, I got the Texas BBQ this time.  It wasn't greasy or too doughy or too spicy, but it hit the spot.

The deal that reeled me in was a small card on my front door, that is good for every order of a Large or Extra Large you can get another of the same  size or smaller for free. I reiterated that I moved in July. The employee shared that there is no way that Bell could have known that I moved if I didn't submit that information in writing. < Text>
I have had Bell Pest Control Service since I purchased my first home in 2014. I recently purchased a new home in February and within the first month I had a large ant infestation in my home after an ant nest was disturbed following yard work that was done before I purchased the home. I haven't had to do any work in the yard yet, so it wasn't me:-) I called the office first thing in the morning hoping someone could come that day before the ants made it into my pantry. I wish I could remember the name of who I spoke with. She was absolutely lovely, sympathetic and went above and beyond to get techs to my house that afternoon. If I recall, she mentioned that she lives in Galt, I hope that helps her supervisor identify her.
Osmand and Isiah arrived that afternoon to spray inside and out, inspected my attic to make sure there were no rodents (as the home inspection noted some old droppings up there) and they inspected the backyard to see where the ants were coming from. Sure enough, Isiah was able to identify the source and followed the ant trail clear across my backyard to my fruit trees. They treated the area and walked me through everything they did before leaving. We set up a follow-up appointment for Osmand to return two-weeks later to check on the bait he placed in the attic and check on the ant situation.
At our follow-up appointment I informed Osmand that I thought there may be a dead rodent in my wall and I had been smelling it since the day I moved in, he also smelt it. He went straight to the attic, checked the old bait and placed an odor absorption bag in my attic to help with the odor as he couldn't find the animal. OMG it has only been an hour and the smell is already improving. He treated the backyard again as there was still a decent ant trail moving along my patio, but luckily no more ants in the house!! WOOHOO
In my opinion, Bell Pest Control is great. I have always lucked out getting truly amazing techs that seem to go above and beyond. They are always so professional, personable and genuine.
Thank You
Alicia<//Text>

We've had Bell for almost 2 years. In that time the techs have been great and we've been happy, until now. In February the tech called and asked if he could come by the next day. I told him we'd have to reschedule as I could not make it home to put the dogs in. The next thing I know Bell is charging me for the service because they say they could not collect payment that day and I refused service?? Ok ok, I figure it was as much my fault as I had forgotten about it. I called in to figure it all out and the lady who answered was probably the rudest person I've ever dealt with. She refused to help me out, refused to give me the service I paid for, and refused to let me cancel. She kept saying I had to give her 30 days written notice and that since I'm up for service this month, I have to pay for both February and April or she would send me to collections that day. I was at a loss for words. I just can't believe customer service has gotten this bad. I am rarely rattled but this person had me rattled. I ended up paying the 2 service fees and getting them out of our lives. Yes, she got what she wanted, but I just can't give my money to a company, a family owned company, that treats their customers this way. Extremely disappointed with our experience in discontinuing our services with Bell Pest Control due to moving out of the property. We are CONTINUING to be charged for services at that property despite following all the proper channels, i.e. written notification requesting cancellation of service, verbal notification on NUMEROUS occasions AND notifying our service person, Steve (who was always great, btw...too bad they don't hire his degree of honesty & integrity in the office), that we had cancelled the services. We ultimately had to file a fraudulant charge claim with our bank against Bell Pest Control in order to rectify the situation, get the charges reversed and prevent them from posting additional charges to our account. **We were treated extremely rudely by their staff members and were basically told "too bad" when they were unable to 'find' our paperwork.

Think twice before using them...do you want to be charged for services not rendered and continue to pay for those services even after you've vacated the property? We'll be making a report to the BBB, as well as informing everyone we know of our experience.

It appears, from the other reviews here, that this is a pattern with Bell Pest Control. Do your homework before signing up...shady business practices do not make for happy customers, nor long-term customers!

Todd and Claudia Speelman</review>
